 ● Advice36.txt highlights clarity improvements for My Account:

     - Replace the six-card “Account Menu” grid with true navigation tabs, moving production timing info into Orders.
     - Introduce a clear page header before Saved Designs to anchor the section.
     - Restructure saved-design cards: emphasize status (Awaiting Approval, Ready to Order, etc.), keep summaries

     - Shrink and make the preview image actionable, place actions near titles.
     - Hide the builder sidebar when viewing account pages; show account navigation instead.
     - Use human-friendly timestamps and add filters (status, recently edited, ready for approval, ordered).
